beginSubroutine: s32'OnActionBeginPre'
  storeValue: Mem(ObjReg5), Mem(ObjReg6)
  storeValue: Mem(ObjReg6), Val(0)
  changeMaterialSet: s32'ChangeColor'
endSubroutine: 

beginSubroutine: s32'OnFrameStep'
  callSubroutine: s32'cmnOnFrameStep'
  exGaugeColor: 0, -16744193
  exGaugeIcon: 0, 1
  getTrainingItemVal: s32'TRP_ZAT', 2, 157
  if: Mem(PlayerVal0)
    ifNot: Mem(PlayerVal3)
      if: Mem(BattleDoing)
        ifNot: Mem(IsSomebodysCutScene)
          ifNot: Mem(IsRoundTimerStop)
            ifNot: Mem(CheckStop)
              ifOperation: (IS_NOT_EQUAL), Mem(TrainingValue), Val(2)
                modifyVar: (ADD), Mem(ExGauge0), Val(-5)
              endIf: 
            endIf: 
          endIf: 
        endIf: 
      endIf: 
    endIf: 
  endIf: 
  else: 
    ifNot: Mem(ObjReg0)
      storeValue: Mem(GTmpReg0), Val(0)
      modifyVar: (OR), Mem(GTmpReg0), Mem(PlayerVal1)
      if: Mem(GTmpReg0)
        ifNot: Mem(IsSomebodysCutScene)
          ifNot: Mem(IsRoundTimerStop)
            ifNot: Mem(CheckStop)
              modifyVar: (ADD), Mem(ExGauge0), Val(15)
              if: Mem(TrainingValue)
                modifyVar: (ADD), Mem(ExGauge0), Val(999999)
              endIf: 
            endIf: 
          endIf: 
        endIf: 
        exGaugeColor: 0, -65536
        exGaugeIcon: 0, 2
      endIf: 
      else: 
        ifNot: Mem(IsSomebodysCutScene)
          ifNot: Mem(IsRoundTimerStop)
            ifNot: Mem(CheckStop)
              modifyVar: (ADD), Mem(ExGauge0), Val(55)
              if: Mem(TrainingValue)
                modifyVar: (ADD), Mem(ExGauge0), Val(999999)
              endIf: 
            endIf: 
          endIf: 
        endIf: 
        exGaugeColor: 0, -1
      endElse: 
    endIf: 
  endElse: 
  ifOperation: (IS_GREATER_OR_EQUAL), Mem(ExGauge0), Val(3000)
    storeValue: Mem(PlayerVal1), Val(0)
  endIf: 
  if: Mem(CmnCharaReg5)
    ifOperation: (IS_LESSER_OR_EQUAL), Mem(PosY), Val(4750000)
      isObjectActive: (STACK0)
      if: Mem(Tmp)
        runOnObject: (STACK0)
          deactivateCurrentObject: 
        endRunOnObject: 
      endIf: 
    endIf: 
    isObjectActive: (STACK0)
    if: Mem(Tmp)
      storeValueFromObject: (SELF), Mem(ObjReg1), (STACK0), Mem(PosY)
    endIf: 
    ifOperation: (IS_LESSER_OR_EQUAL), Mem(ObjReg1), Val(5500000)
      isObjectActive: (STACK0)
      if: Mem(Tmp)
        runOnObject: (STACK0)
          recoveryState: 
        endRunOnObject: 
      endIf: 
    endIf: 
    ifOperation: (IS_LESSER_OR_EQUAL), Mem(ObjReg1), Val(5000000)
      isObjectActive: (STACK0)
      if: Mem(Tmp)
        runOnObject: (STACK0)
          deactivateCurrentObject: 
        endRunOnObject: 
      endIf: 
    endIf: 
  endIf: 
  if: Mem(CheckStop)
    storeValue: Mem(PlayerVal2), Val(1)
  endIf: 
  else: 
    storeValue: Mem(PlayerVal2), Val(0)
  endElse: 
endSubroutine:

  sprite: s32'zat021_19', 3

  gotoIfOperation: s32'FJumpLandingTurn', (IS_LESSER_OR_EQUAL), Mem(EnemyFrontDistance), Val(0)
  sprite: s32'zat021_21', 3
  sprite: s32'zat021_22', 3

beginState: s32'CmnActAirFDash'
  upon: (IMMEDIATE)
    setCommonActionMark: 1
    upon: (IDLING)
      ifNot: Mem(ActReg0)
        ifOperation: (IS_GREATER_OR_EQUAL), Mem(SpeedY), Val(1)
          ifOperation: (IS_LESSER_OR_EQUAL), Mem(ActionTime), Val(5)
            velocityYPercent: 95
          endIf: 
          else: 
            ifOperation: (IS_LESSER_OR_EQUAL), Mem(ActionTime), Val(17)
              physicsYImpulse: 0, 0
              setGravity: 0
            endIf: 
          endElse: 
        endIf: 
        else: 
          physicsYImpulse: 0, 0
          setGravity: 0
        endElse: 
      endIf: 
      ifOperation: (IS_EQUAL), Mem(ActionTime), Val(13)
        createParticle: s32'cmn_air_dash', (HEAD)
        cmnSfx: s32'SE_BTL_CMN_DashAir'
        setMotionBlurAmount: 150
      endIf: 
      ifOperation: (IS_EQUAL), Mem(ActionTime), Val(17)
        resetMotionBlurAmount: 
      endIf: 
      if: Mem(ActReg0)
        checkInput: (INPUT_ANY_UP)
        if: Mem(Tmp)
          addVelocityY: 0, 1000
        endIf: 
        checkInput: (INPUT_ANY_DOWN)
        if: Mem(Tmp)
          addVelocityY: 0, -1000
        endIf: 
      endIf: 
    endUpon: 
    upon: (BEFORE_EXIT)
      resetGravity: 
    endUpon: 
  endUpon: 
  sprite: s32'zat351_08', 3
  physicsXImpulse: 0, 20000
  velocityXRate: 25
  sprite: s32'zat351_07', 3
  physicsYImpulse: 0, 0
  setGravity: 0
  sprite: s32'zat351_06', 3
  sprite: s32'zat351_05', 3

beginState: s32'HomingJump'
  upon: (IMMEDIATE)
    callSubroutine: s32'cmn_Dust_HomingJump'
    storeValue: Mem(ActReg2), Val(250000)
    storeValue: Mem(ActReg3), Val(250000)
    storeValue: Mem(ActReg4), Val(-15000)
    storeValue: Mem(ActReg5), Val(100000)
    storeValue: Mem(ActReg6), Val(50000)
    upon: (TIMER)
      upon: (IDLING)
        modifyVar: (ADD), Mem(ActReg0), Val(50)
        ifOperation: (IS_GREATER_OR_EQUAL), Mem(ActReg0), Val(1000)
          storeValue: Mem(ActReg0), Val(1000)
        endIf: 
        modifyVar: (ADD), Mem(ActReg1), Val(1)
        ifOperation: (IS_LESSER_OR_EQUAL), Mem(ActReg1), Val(6)
          ifOperation: (IS_LESSER_OR_EQUAL), Mem(ActReg1), Val(3)
            spriteBlend: s32'zat035_04', 2, 45
          endIf: 
          else: 
            spriteBlend: s32'zat035_05', 2, 45
            ifOperation: (IS_GREATER_OR_EQUAL), Mem(ActReg1), Val(6)
              storeValue: Mem(ActReg1), Val(0)
            endIf: 
          endElse: 
        endIf: 
      endUpon: 
    endUpon: 
    storeValue: Mem(PlayerVal6), Val(1)
  endUpon: 
  sprite: s32'zat205_06', 5
  displayMesh: s32'zatw_HammerBoots', 1
  displayMesh: s32'Edyw_edyeye', 1
  createObject: s32'Dashbrake', (BACK_2_BODY)

  if: Mem(Tmp)
    runOnObject: (STACK0)
      linkObjPosition: 3
    endRunOnObject: 
  endIf: 
  sprite: s32'zat205_07', 5
  sprite: s32'zat205_08', 5
  sprite: s32'zat205_09', 1
